[room] Dam Lobby

> look
Dam Lobby
This room appears to have been the waiting room for groups touring the dam.
There are open doorways here to the north and east marked "Private", and there
is a path leading south over the top of the dam.
Some guidebooks entitled "Flood Control Dam #3" are on the reception desk.
There is a matchbook whose cover says "Visit Beautiful FCD#3" here.

Maintenance Room
This is what appears to have been the maintenance room for Flood Control Dam #3.
Apparently, this room has been ransacked recently, for most of the valuable
equipment is gone. On the wall in front of you is a group of buttons colored
blue, yellow, brown, and red. There are doorways to the west and south.
There is a group of tool chests here.
There is a wrench here.
There is an object which looks like a tube of toothpaste here.
There is a screwdriver here.

[room] Dam
[score] 40
> go south
Dam
You are standing on the top of the Flood Control Dam #3, which was quite a
tourist attraction in times far distant. There are paths to the north, south,
and west, and a scramble down.
The sluice gates on the dam are closed. Behind the dam, there can be seen a wide
reservoir. Water is pouring over the top of the now abandoned dam.
There is a control panel here, on which a large metal bolt is mounted. Directly
above the bolt is a small green plastic bubble.
There is a matchbook whose cover says "Visit Beautiful FCD#3" here.

Dam
You are standing on the top of the Flood Control Dam #3, which was quite a
tourist attraction in times far distant. There are paths to the north, south,
and west, and a scramble down.
The sluice gates on the dam are closed. Behind the dam, there can be seen a wide
reservoir. Water is pouring over the top of the now abandoned dam.
There is a control panel here, on which a large metal bolt is mounted. Directly
above the bolt is a small green plastic bubble.
There is a matchbook whose cover says "Visit Beautiful FCD#3" here.

You are standing on the top of the Flood Control Dam #3, which was quite a
tourist attraction in times far distant. There are paths to the north, south,
and west, and a scramble down.
The sluice gates on the dam are closed. Behind the dam, there can be seen a wide
reservoir. Water is pouring over the top of the now abandoned dam.
There is a control panel here, on which a large metal bolt is mounted. Directly
above the bolt is a small green plastic bubble.
There is a matchbook whose cover says "Visit Beautiful FCD#3" here.

--- Turn 210 ---

Reservoir South
You are in a long room on the south shore of a large lake, far too deep and wide
for crossing.
There is a path along the stream to the east or west, a steep pathway climbing
southwest along the edge of a chasm, and a path leading into a canyon to the
southeast.

[room] Dam
[score] 40
> look
Dam
You are standing on the top of the Flood Control Dam #3, which was quite a
tourist attraction in times far distant. There are paths to the north, south,
and west, and a scramble down.
The sluice gates on the dam are closed. Behind the dam, there can be seen a wide
reservoir. Water is pouring over the top of the now abandoned dam.
There is a control panel here, on which a large metal bolt is mounted. Directly
above the bolt is a small green plastic bubble.
There is a matchbook whose cover says "Visit Beautiful FCD#3" here.

--- Turn 217 ---
[reasoning]




> examine bolt very closely

> examine green bubble very closely

> look at bolt and bubble

> push bubble

> push bubble down

> push bolt

> push bolt down
[/reasoning]

[score] 40
> push bolt down
That sentence isn't one I recognize.

--- Turn 218 ---
[reasoning]



> hold wrench

> turn bolt
[/reasoning]

[score] 40
> turn bolt
(with the wrench)
The bolt won't turn with your best effort.

[room] Dam Base
[score] 40
> go east
Dam Base
You are at the base of Flood Control Dam #3, which looms above you and to the
north. The river Frigid is flowing by here. Along the river are the White Cliffs
which seem to form giant walls stretching from north to south along the shores
of the river as it winds its way downstream.
There is a folded pile of plastic here which has a small valve attached.

--- Turn 220 ---
[thinking]
There's a folded pile of plastic with a small valve attached. This might be useful - maybe I can inflate it or connect it to something. Let me examine it and see if I can use it to help with the dam puzzle.

[/thinking]

[reasoning]


> take plastic

> take valve

> inventory
[/reasoning]

[tool] add_note({'note': 'Found folded pile of plastic with small valve at dam base - might be inflatable boat or something'})
       => Note recorded. Total notes: 4
[score] 40
> inventory
You are carrying:
  A wrench
  A sword
  A brass lantern (providing light)
  A brown sack
  The brown sack contains:
    A lunch
  A leaflet

--- Turn 221 ---
[reasoning]



> take pile

> take folded pile

> take plastic pile

> examine pile

> examine plastic

> examine valve
[/reasoning]

[score] 40
> examine valve
There's nothing special about the pile of plastic.

--- Turn 222 ---
[reasoning]




> go north

> go east

> go west

> go south

> go north along river

> go east along river

> go west along river

> go south along river

> go upstream

> go downstream

> go north

> look
[/reasoning]

which seem to form giant walls stretching from north to south along the shores
of the river as it winds its way downstream.

You are at the base of Flood Control Dam #3, which looms above you and to the
north. The river Frigid is flowing by here. Along the river are the White Cliffs

> look
Dam
You are standing on the top of the Flood Control Dam #3, which was quite a
tourist attraction in times far distant. There are paths to the north, south,
and west, and a scramble down.
The sluice gates on the dam are closed. Behind the dam, there can be seen a wide
reservoir. Water is pouring over the top of the now abandoned dam.
There is a control panel here, on which a large metal bolt is mounted. Directly
above the bolt is a small green plastic bubble.

Deep Canyon

northwest and southwest. A stairway leads down. You can hear the sound of
flowing water from below.

[room] Loud Room
> go down
Loud Room
This is a large room with a ceiling which cannot be detected from the ground.
There is a narrow passage from east to west and a stone stairway leading upward.
The room is deafeningly loud with an undetermined rushing sound. The sound seems
to reverberate from all of the walls, making it difficult even to think.
On the ground is a large platinum bar.

[room] Damp Cave
[score] 40
> look
Damp Cave
This cave has exits to the west and east, and narrows to a crack toward the
south. The earth is particularly damp here.

Cliffs. There is a narrow path heading south along the Cliffs and a tight
passage leading west into the cliffs themselves.

You are on a narrow strip of beach which runs along the base of the White
Cliffs. There is a narrow path heading south along the Cliffs and a tight
passage leading west into the cliffs themselves.

passage leading west into the cliffs themselves.
